Sportradar Soccer v4 Documentation
Sportradar's Soccer API provides real-time game updates and a vast database of supplementary statistics for the largest leagues in the world. Data is collected via Sportradar on-venue scouts and in-house operators. Over 650 unique competitions are available in one package.

The Soccer API is consistent in structure, format and behavior with the other General Sport APIs. Primary feeds will return seasons, competitions, team/player data and real-time scores.

Additional feeds provide a host of complimentary stats, including:

Live standings for top leagues
League leaders
Win probabilities for every match
Lineups with formations
Seasonal statistics
Season leaders
Missing/Injured players
Live ball-spotting data (x,y coordinates for events on the field)
Head-to-head statistics
Fun facts
Real-time customers are also offered two delivery Push Feeds to enhance speed.

An extra package containing extended statistics is also available. This package includes live extended match player stats for:

Minutes
Passing
Tackles
Crosses
Blocks/Saves
Fouls
Offsides
An extended Probabilities package is also offered. This add-on includes in-game probability updates and season outrights.

The easiest way to get started with the API is to click the fork button to fork this collection to your own workspace and use Postman to send requests.

To receive trial access, visit this page.

Authorization
API Key
Key
x-api-key
Value
<value>
Probabilities Package
This collection of probability feeds is available for licensing as an add-on feature. They are an extension of the Season Probabilities feed in the main package which provides pre-match probabilities for the sport event winner market.

Probability packages are for media use only. Use of this API is prohibited for betting clients.

The main features of the Probabilities extension (where coverage applies) are:

Live Probabilities that update throughout game
Season Outright Probabilities for the Tournament Winner market
Live Probabilities Coverage indicator for the next 24 hours
For more information or to request a Trial of this feature, please contact a Sportradar Sales representative at us-sales@sportradar.com.

Authorization
API Key
This folder is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
GET
Live Probabilities
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer-probabilities/trial/v4/en/schedules/live/probabilities.json
Provides top-level information for live matches. If probabilities are available for a match, pre-match and live probabilities will be displayed.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
GET
Season Outright Probabilities
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer-probabilities/trial/v4/en/seasons/:season_id/outright_probabilities.json
Provides a list of outright probabilities for each competitor from a given season.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
season_id
sr:season:84048
ID of a season

Sport Event Probabilities
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer-probabilities/trial/v4/en/sport_events/:sport_event_id/sport_event_probabilities.json
Provides pre-match and live probabilities for a given match.

Sport Event Timeline Probabilities
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer-probabilities/trial/v4/en/sport_events/:sport_event_id/timeline_probabilities.json
Provides a timeline of pre-match and live probability changes for a given match. This also provides match information including player stats, team stats, and scoring info.

Competition Info
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/competitions/:urn_competition/info.json
Provides the name, id, and parent id for a given competition.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_competition
sr:competition:17
(Required) Competition URN (sr:competition:x)

OK
Request

GET
Competitor Mappings
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/competitors/mappings.json?offset=0&start=5&limit=5
Provides competitor id mapping between previous versions of the Soccer API.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Query Params
offset
0
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

start
5
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

limit
5
The numbers of items to return. Maximum: 200

Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/competitors/mappings.json?offset=0&start=5&limit=5&api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK
Response
Body

GET
Competitor vs Competitor
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/competitors/:urn_competitor/versus/:urn_competitor2/summaries.json
Provides previous and upcoming matches between two teams including scoring information, player and team match statistics.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_competitor
sr:competitor:17
(Required) Competitor URN (sr:competitor:x)

urn_competitor2
sr:competitor:42
(Required) Competitor 2 URN (sr:competitor:x)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/competitors/sr:competitor:17/versus/sr:competitor:42/summaries.json?api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK
Response
Body

GET
Daily Summaries
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/schedules/:urn_date/summaries.json?offset=0&limit=5
Provides match information for a given day including team scoring, player and team match statistics.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Query Params
offset
0
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

limit
5
The numbers of items to return. Maximum: 200

Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_date
2019-03-21
(Required) Date (YYYY-MM-DD)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/schedules/2019-03-21/summaries.json?offset=0&limit=5&api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK
Response
Body

GET
Live Summaries
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/schedules/live/summaries.json
Provides match information for all currently live matches including team scoring, player and team match statistics. This feed updates in real time as matches are played. Matches appear a few minutes before kick-off and disappear a few minutes after the match reaches “ended” status.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/schedules/live/summaries.json?api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK

GET
Live Timelines
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/schedules/live/timelines.json
Provides a play-by-play event timeline for currently live matches. Matches appear a few minutes before kick-off and disappear a few minutes after the match reaches “ended” status.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/schedules/live/timelines.json?api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK
Response
Body
Headers (1)

GET
Player Mappings
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/players/mappings.json?offset=0&start=5&limit=5
Provides player id mapping between previous versions of the Soccer API.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Query Params
offset
0
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

start
5
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

limit
5
The numbers of items to return. Maximum: 200

Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/players/mappings.json?offset=0&start=5&limit=5&api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK

GET
Player Merge Mappings
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/players/merge_mappings.json

GET
Season Competitors
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/seasons/:urn_season/competitors.json?offset=0&limit=5&start=5
Provides a list of teams participating for a given season.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Query Params
offset
0
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

limit
5
The numbers of items to return. Maximum: 200

start
5
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_season
sr:season:66441
(Required) Season URN (sr:season:x)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/seasons/sr:season:54571/competitors.json?offset=0&limit=5&start=5&api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK
Response
Body
Headers (4)
View More
json

GET
Season Form Standings
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/seasons/:urn_season/form_standings.json
Provides a form table of game results and splits for a given season. Table displays W/D/L (win/draw/loss) for a maximum of 6 matches for each team.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Query Params
round
2
Standings for specified round number. If the round number is not specified, last round is displayed by default.

Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_season
sr:season:66441
(Required) Season URN (sr:season:x)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/seasons/sr:season:54571/standings.json?round=2&api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK
Response

GET
Season Info
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/seasons/:urn_season/info.json
Provides detailed information for a given season, including participating teams and coverage level.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_season
sr:season:66441
(Required) Season URN (sr:season:x)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/seasons/sr:season:54571/info.json?api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK

GET
Season Lineups

Provides match lineups and substitutions for a given season.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Query Params
offset
0
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

start
5
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

limit
5
The numbers of items to return. Maximum: 200

locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_season
sr:season:66441
(Required) Season URN (sr:season:x)

GET
Season Schedule
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/seasons/:urn_season/schedules.json
Provides basic match information for all matches for a given season, including scoring and match coverage.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Query Params
limit
0
The numbers of items to return. Maximum: 1000

start
0
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_season
sr:season:66441
(Required) Season URN (sr:season:x)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/seasons/sr:season:54571/schedules.json?api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK
Response
Body

GET
Season Summaries
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/seasons/:urn_season/summaries.json?offset=0&limit=5&start=5
Provides information for all matches from a given season including scoring and statistics at the match level.

This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4

0

start
5
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_season

GET
Season Transfers
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/seasons/:urn_season/transfers.json
Provides a list of all player transfers for a given season.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_season
sr:season:83706
(Required) Season URN (sr:season:x)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/seasons/sr:season:54571/schedules.json?api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'

GET
Sport Event Summary
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/sport_events/:urn_sport_event/summary.json
Provides real-time match-level statistics for a given match. Including player and team stats, scoring info, and channel availability. Please note that data returned is determined by coverage level.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_sport_event
sr:sport_event:18427316
(Required) Sport Event URN (sr:sport_event:x)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/sport_events/sr:sport_event:17693932/summary.json?api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK

GET
Sport Event Timeline
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/sport_events/:urn_sport_event/timeline.json
Provides real-time match-level statistics and a play-by-play event timeline for a given match. This includes player and team stats, scoring info, channel availability, x/y event coordinates, and human-readable event descriptions. Please note that data returned is determined by coverage level.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Path Variables
locale
en
(Required) Locale used for translations

urn_sport_event
sr:sport_event:18427316
(Required) Sport Event URN (sr:sport_event:x)

Example
OK
Request
View More
cURL
curl --location 'https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/en/sport_events/sr:sport_event:17693932/timeline.json?api_key=%3CAPI%20Key%3E'
200 OK
Response

GET
Sport Events Created
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/sport_events/created.json?offset=0&start=5&limit=5
Provides ids for sport events that have been created in the last 24 hours.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4
Query Params
offset
0
The number of items to skip before starting to collect the result set. Default: 0

start
5

GET
Sport Events Removed
https://api.sportradar.com/soccer/trial/v4/:locale/sport_events/removed.json?offset=0&start=5&limit=5
Provides ids for sport events that have been removed from the API.

Authorization
API Key
This request is using an authorization helper from collection Sportradar Soccer v4

0
